         <div class=" ddc-content content-default" data-widget-id="content1" data-widget-name="content-default">
          <h3 class="h1 ddc-heading-1 widget-heading">
           Welcome to Toyota Carlsbad
          </h3>
          <div class="content">
           <div itemscope="" itemtype="//www.schema.org/AutoDealer">
            <h2>
             Welcome to
             <span itemprop="brand">
              Toyota
             </span>
             Carlsbad
             <br/>
             <span itemprop="name">
              Toyota Carlsbad
             </span>
             Happily Serves San Diego, Oceanside, Escondido and San Marcos
            </h2>
            <span itemprop="description">
             <p>
              Whether you're an experienced automotive connoisseur curious about Toyota's latest fleet of critically acclaimed vehicles, or a first-time buyer eager to get behind the wheel of your first car, the Toyota Carlsbad team is thankful for your visit. Over the years, Toyota Carlsbad has managed to set itself apart from other dealerships in order to become the
              <a href="/dealership/toyota-dealer-near-san-diego.htm" internallink="true" target="_self" title="San Diego">
               San Diego
              </a>
              ,
              <a href="/dealership/toyota-dealer-serving-vista.htm" internallink="true" target="_self" title="Vista">
               Vista
              </a>
              , Oceanside,
              <a href="/dealership/toyota-dealer-near-escondido.htm" internallink="true" target="_self" title="Escondido">
               Escondido
              </a>
              and San Marcos region's home for all things automotive.
             </p>
            </span>
            <p>
             It's more than the incredible style, efficient performance and futuristic technology infused in every new Toyota car, truck and SUV. It's also our dedication to our customers. Our staff is comprised of a variety of people who, like you, have lived and worked in the greater-San Diego region for years, so we can appreciate what a great place it is to live and work. Whether it's taking the anxiety out of financing your next vehicle, or helping you with a major repair to your current car, the team here at Toyota Carlsbad aims to reflect the amicability, trustworthiness and sense of humor for which San Diego is known worldwide.
            </p>
            <p>
             Whether you're shopping for an off-road read pickup truck or family-oriented crossover, Toyota Carlsbad is proud to have every
             <a href="/new-inventory/index.htm">
              new Toyota
             </a>
             from the brand's latest model year on hand for you. And if you're looking to harness the power and efficiency of Toyota for less, you're bound to find a vehicle in our constantly-updated inventory of
             <b>
              pre-owned Toyota vehicles.
             </b>
             . We also carry hundreds of vehicles from non-Toyota brands you know.
            </p>
            <h3>
             Stop by Our Auto Finance, Service, or Parts Centers
            </h3>
            <p>
             At Toyota Carlsbad, our selection doesn't end with our terrific inventory of vehicles. Thanks to our relationship with a secure network of banks and lending institutions nationwide, our team also works to help get you the ideal
             <b>
              loan or Toyota lease
             </b>
             package for the vehicle you want. That means little-to-know down payments, reasonable interest rates and low monthly payments that won't impinge on your future financial goals.
            </p>
            <p>
             No matter if you need an assist with the routine maintenance that will keep your Toyota car, truck or SUV running great as long as you own it, or have endured damage to your vehicle on the road, the knowledgeable
             <b>
              parts and service
             </b>
             experts here at Toyota Carlsbad will be here for you. We even offer you an online service scheduler so you can have your oil change, tire rotation, brake replacement or auto body repair done in adherence to your schedule - not ours.
            </p>
            <p>
             We welcome drivers from across San Diego, from
             <a href="/military-rebate.htm">
              military service men and women
             </a>
             to
             <a href="/graduate-rebate.htm">
              recent college graduates
             </a>
             to visit the expansive Toyota Carlsbad showroom today at
             <span itemprop="address">
              5424 Paseo Del Norte Carlsbad, California
             </span>
             . You can even get point-by-point directions from your home or office when you utilize our interactive map. Questions about a vehicle in our inventory, new Toyota incentive program? Send us an e-mail and we'll get back to you shortly. We look forward to meeting you and your family soon.
            </p>
           </div>
          </div>

 $(function() {
 var vehicleId = "",
 summarySessionStorage = 'drSummary',
 enablePercentIndicator = false;
 if(DDC.WidgetData && DDC.WidgetData["digital_retailing_default"] && DDC.WidgetData["digital_retailing_default"].prefs["enablePercentIndicator"]) {
 enablePercentIndicator = DDC.WidgetData["digital_retailing_default"].prefs["enablePercentIndicator"];
 }
 setTabSummary = function(tabName,complete) {
 DDC.digitalRetailing.summary[tabName].complete = complete;
 if(tabName == 'payment' || tabName == 'reserve'|| tabName == 'accessories'){
 DDC.digitalRetailing.summary[tabName].vehicleComplete = complete;
 }
 }
 processTabs = function(tabName){
 switch (tabName) {
 case 'trade':
 if(DDC.userProfile.ownedVehicle && DDC.userProfile.ownedVehicle.valuations && DDC.userProfile.ownedVehicle.valuations.length > 0){
 setTabSummary(tabName,true);
 }
 break;
 case 'accessories':
 if(DDC.userProfile.vehicleAccessories && DDC.userProfile.vehicleAccessories[vehicleId] && DDC.userProfile.vehicleAccessories[vehicleId].accessoriesTotal != null && DDC.userProfile.vehicleAccessories[vehicleId].accessoriesTotal != undefined){
 setTabSummary(tabName,true);
 }
 break;
 case 'payment':
 if(DDC.userProfile.paymentQuotes && DDC.userProfile.paymentQuotes[vehicleId]){
 setTabSummary(tabName,true);
 }
 break;
 case 'prequal':
 if( (DDC.userProfile.preQualification && DDC.userProfile.preQualification.referenceNumber) || (DDC.userProfile.creditApplication && DDC.userProfile.creditApplication.referenceNumber) ){
 setTabSummary(tabName,true);
 }
 break;
 case 'finance':
 if(DDC.userProfile.creditApplication && DDC.userProfile.creditApplication.referenceNumber){
 setTabSummary(tabName,true);
 }
 break;
 case 'reserve':
 if(DDC.userProfile.vehicleReservations && DDC.userProfile.vehicleReservations[vehicleId]) {
 setTabSummary(tabName,true);
 }
 break;
 case 'protect':
 if(DDC.userProfile.protectionPlan) {
 setTabSummary(tabName,true);
 }
 break;
 case 'lifestyle':
 if(DDC.userProfile.progress && DDC.userProfile.progress.INLINE_DR_MENU){
 setTabSummary(tabName,true);
 }
 break;
 case 'pickup':
 if(DDC.userProfile.progress && DDC.userProfile.progress.INLINE_DR_PICKUP){
 setTabSummary(tabName,true);
 }
 break;
 case 'testdrive':
 if(DDC.userProfile.progress && DDC.userProfile.progress.INLINE_DR_TESTDRIVE){
 setTabSummary(tabName,true);
 }
 break;
 default:
 break;
 }
 }
 calculatePercentComplete = function(){
 if(enablePercentIndicator) {
 var totalTools = Object.keys(DDC.digitalRetailing.summary).length,
 completedToolsGlobal = 0,
 completedToolsVehicle = 0,
 publishPercentUpdate = false;
 for (var tool in DDC.digitalRetailing.summary) {
 if(tool == 'payment' || tool == 'reserve' || tool == 'accessories') {
 if(DDC.digitalRetailing.summary[tool].complete == true){
 completedToolsGlobal++
 }
 if(DDC.digitalRetailing.summary[tool].vehicleComplete == true){
 completedToolsVehicle++
 }
 } else if (DDC.digitalRetailing.summary[tool].complete == true) {
 completedToolsGlobal++
 completedToolsVehicle++
 }
 }
 var percentGlobalComplete = completedToolsGlobal / totalTools,
 percentVehicleComplete = completedToolsVehicle / totalTools;
 if (DDC.digitalRetailing.percentGlobalComplete != percentGlobalComplete) {
 DDC.digitalRetailing.percentGlobalComplete = percentGlobalComplete;
 publishPercentUpdate = true;
 }
 if (DDC.digitalRetailing.percentVehicleComplete != percentVehicleComplete) {
 DDC.digitalRetailing.percentVehicleComplete = percentVehicleComplete;
 publishPercentUpdate = true;
 }
 if(publishPercentUpdate) {
 jQuery.publish('dr-percentComplete-updated');
 }
 }
 }
 if (!DDC.digitalRetailing.summary["trade"]) {
 DDC.digitalRetailing.summary["trade"] = {'text': "Value a Trade", 'time': "30 minutes", 'complete': false};
 }
 processTabs("trade");
 jQuery.subscribe("dr-trade-complete", function() {
 setTabSummary("trade",true);
 calculatePercentComplete();
 sessionStorage.setItem(summarySessionStorage, JSON.stringify(DDC.digitalRetailing));
 });
 jQuery.subscribe('mycars-user-logging-out', function(){
 setTabSummary("trade",false);
